########################
## Sichuan Focus Tree ##
## By Alpinia         ##
########################

focus_tree = {
	id = sichuan_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = SZC
		}
	}
	default = no
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 2600 y = 950 }

	### Generic Post Unification ###
	shared_focus = CHS_provisional_government
	shared_focus = CHS_reintegrate_academies
	shared_focus = CHS_standardised_arsenals
	shared_focus = CHS_southern_fleets_legacy

	### Federalist Post Unification ###
	#Election related stuff
	shared_focus = UPC_affairs_of_the_ruling_coalition
	shared_focus = UPC_calls_for_a_constitutional_convention

	#Foreign Policy Tree
	shared_focus = CHN_return_to_the_world_stage_focus

	### Table of Contents ###
	# Economic Tree

	# Shared Military Tree
	# Zhili Military Tree
	# Baoding/Officer Department Military Tree
	# Accelerated Military Tree

	# Armament Political Focus Tree
	# Baoding Department Political Tree
	# Accelerated Department Political Tree
	# Officer Department Focus Tree
	# Federalist Bastion Tree
	# Zhili Remnant Tree

### Economic Tree ###
	focus = {
		id = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_railroad
		cost = 5

		x = 17
		y = 0

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_internal_divisions }
				NOT = { has_idea = SZC_internal_divisions }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea }
				NOT = { has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { SZC_war_aftermath_active = yes }
				SZC_war_aftermath_active = no
			}
			605 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			650 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		offset = {
			x = -1
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = SZC_baoding_department_in_power
					has_country_flag = SZC_officer_department_in_power
				}
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -30
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = SZC_federalists_in_power
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -3
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = SZC_accelerated_department_in_power
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 20 }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway"
			605 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				if = {
					limit = { free_building_slots = { building = infrastructure size > 0 } }
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			650 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				if = {
					limit = { free_building_slots = { building = infrastructure size > 0 } }
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			build_railway = {
				level = 1
				start_province = 4925
				target_province = 6999
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
				bonus = 2
				uses = 1
				category = train_tech
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
	}

	focus = {
		id = SZC_New_Commercial_Zones
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_positive_trade_relations_gold
		cost = 4

		relative_position_id = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
		x = -3
		y = 1

		available = {
			SZC_opium_tier_1_unlocked = yes
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 5 }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_New_Commercial_Zones"
			add_ideas = SZC_commercial_expansion_1
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			add_one_random_civilian_factory = yes
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = SZC_The_Yangtze_Lifeline
		icon = GFX_goal_bluewater_navy
		cost = 4

		relative_position_id = SZC_New_Commercial_Zones
		x = -1
		y = 1

		available = {
			SZC_opium_tier_1_unlocked = yes
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = SZC_New_Commercial_Zones
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 10 }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_The_Yangtze_Lifeline"
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_3
					add_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_4
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_1
					add_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc_aat = no }
				custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
				show_ideas_tooltip = minsheng_shipping
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { mio:CHN_naval_industry_organisation = { is_mio_available = no } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = available_mio_tt
					show_mio_tooltip = CHN_naval_industry_organisation
				}
				mio:CHN_naval_industry_organisation = {
					set_mio_flag = CHN_mio_unlocked
					add_mio_size = 1
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
	}

				limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_3
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_4
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has heavy fire tactics
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_5 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_5
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_7
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has increased munitions production

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has heavy fire tactics and increased munitions production
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_9 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_9
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_10
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_1
					add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_2
				}
			}

				}
			}
			else_if = { #has firepower
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_3
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_10
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has logistics and operations
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_5 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_5
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_12
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has logistics and firepower
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_6 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_6
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_13
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has operations and firepower
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_8 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_8
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_14
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has logistics, operations and firepower
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_11 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_11
					add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_15
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = SZC_industrial_army_4
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
	}

				limit = { has_idea = SZC_nonsensical_economic_situation_2 }
				remove_ideas = SZC_nonsensical_economic_situation_2
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_nonsensical_economic_situation_1
					add_idea = SZC_nonsensical_economic_situation_2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
				add_ideas = SZC_chinas_industrial_revolution
				add_one_random_civilian_factory = yes
				add_one_random_military_factory = yes
				add_one_random_infrastructure = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SZC_government_union_partnership
					days = 330
				}
				add_stability = 0.03
				UPC_KMT_medium_effect = yes
				UPC_CSP_medium_effect = yes
				UPC_RAD_small_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
